 from svn_to_muse import model_config

 # 全局日志目录
 _log_dir: Optional[str] = None


 def set_log_dir(log_dir: str) -> None:
     """设置日志目录"""
     global _log_dir
     _log_dir = log_dir
     if not os.path.exists(_log_dir):
         os.makedirs(_log_dir)


 def log_export(skeleton_name: str, anim_name: str, status: str, message: str = "", duration: float = 0) -> None:
     """
     记录动画导出日志

     Args:
         skeleton_name: 骨骼名称
         anim_name: 动画名称
         status: 状态（success/failed/timeout）
         message: 附加消息
         duration: 导出耗时（秒）
     """
     if not _log_dir:
         return

     timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
     log_entry = {
         "timestamp": timestamp,
         "skeleton": skeleton_name,
         "animation": anim_name,
         "status": status,
         "message": message,
         "duration": duration,
     }

     # 按日期创建日志文件
     date_str = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d")
     log_file = os.path.join(_log_dir, f"export_{date_str}.log")

     # 追加日志
     with open(log_file, "a", encoding="utf-8") as f:
         f.write(json.dumps(log_entry, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")


 LOGGER = logging.getLogger("Svn2Muse")

   # 💡 LOGGER=<Logger Svn2Muse (WARNING)> (Logger)
 H74_SVN_DIR_ID = 434397850042369

   # 💡 H74_SVN_DIR_ID=434397850042369 (int)
 def read_scan_cache(scan_cache_file: str) -> Tuple[Dict[str, List[str]], Dict[str, List[Dict[str, Any]]]]:
     with open(scan_cache_file, "r") as f:
         data = json.load(f)
     anims_data: Dict[str, List[str]] = {}
     anim_data = data.get("SkeletonAnimation")
     LOGGER.info("anim_data count: {}".format(len(anim_data)))

     # Skeleton data
     skeleton_data: Dict[str, List[Dict[str, Any]]] = {}
     for anim in anim_data:
         skeleton_path = anim.get("path")
         if not skeleton_path:
             continue

         anims_data.setdefault(anim.get("res"), []).append(skeleton_path)

         skeleton_path = skeleton_path.rsplit("/", 1)[0]

         if skeleton_path in skeleton_data:
             skeleton_data[skeleton_path].append(anim)
         else:
             skeleton_data[skeleton_path] = [anim]

     # skeleton data export fbx
     # anims data upload muse
     return anims_data, skeleton_data


 def batch_run_cmds_file(cmds_file: str) -> None:
     with open(cmds_file, "r") as f:
         cmds = f.readlines()
     batch_run_cmds(cmds)


 def run_single_cmd(cmd: str, timeout_seconds: int = 360, skeleton_name: str = "", anim_names: Optional[List[str]] = None) -> Tuple[str, bool, str]:
     """
     执行单个命令（用于多进程）

     Args:
         cmd: 命令字符串
         timeout_seconds: 超时时间（秒）
         skeleton_name: 骨骼名称（用于日志）
         anim_names: 动画名称列表（用于日志）

     Returns:
         (cmd, success, message)
     """
     import time

     start_time = time.time()

     try:
         print("[执行] {}".format(cmd[:100] + "..." if len(cmd) > 100 else cmd))
         # 使用CREATE_NEW_CONSOLE创建新控制台窗口，同时捕获输出以便监控
         process = subprocess.Popen(
             cmd,
             shell=True,
             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
             stderr=subprocess.STDOUT,
             text=True,
             bufsize=1,
             encoding='utf-8',
             errors='replace',
             creationflags=subprocess.CREATE_NEW_CONSOLE
         )

         # 启动输出监控线程（在后台读取输出，避免阻塞）
         import threading
         def read_output():
             try:
                 while True:
                     line = process.stdout.readline()
                     if not line:
                         break
                     line = line.rstrip()
                     if line:
                         print(f"[输出] {line}")
             except Exception:
                 pass

         output_thread = threading.Thread(target=read_output, daemon=True)
         output_thread.start()

         try:
             returncode = process.wait(timeout=timeout_seconds)
             duration = time.time() - start_time

             if returncode == 0:
                 print("[完成] 命令执行成功，耗时: {:.2f} 秒".format(duration))
                 # 记录成功日志
                 if anim_names:
                     for anim_name in anim_names:
                         log_export(
                             skeleton_name, anim_name, "success", "导出成功", duration
                         )
                 return (cmd, True, "成功")
             else:
                 print(
                     "[失败] 命令返回错误代码: {}，耗时: {:.2f} 秒".format(
                         returncode, duration
                     )
                 )
                 # 记录失败日志
                 if anim_names:
                     for anim_name in anim_names:
                         log_export(
                             skeleton_name,
                             anim_name,
                             "failed",
                             f"错误代码: {returncode}",
                             duration,
                         )
                 return (cmd, False, "错误代码: {}".format(returncode))
         except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
             duration = time.time() - start_time
             print("[超时] 命令执行超过 {} 秒，终止进程".format(timeout_seconds))
             process.kill()
             process.wait()
             # 记录超时日志
             if anim_names:
                 for anim_name in anim_names:
                     log_export(
                         skeleton_name,
                         anim_name,
                         "timeout",
                         f"超时 ({timeout_seconds}秒)",
                         duration,
                     )
             return (cmd, False, "超时")
     except Exception as e:
         duration = time.time() - start_time
         print("[错误] {}".format(str(e)))
         # 记录错误日志
         if anim_names:
             for anim_name in anim_names:
                 log_export(skeleton_name, anim_name, "error", str(e), duration)
         return (cmd, False, str(e))


 def batch_run_cmds(cmds: List[str], timeout_seconds: int = 360) -> None:
     """
     批量执行命令（串行），每个命令有超时限制

     Args:
         cmds: 命令列表
         timeout_seconds: 每个命令的超时时间（秒），默认 360 秒（3 分钟）
     """
     for cmd in cmds:
         run_single_cmd(cmd, timeout_seconds)


 def batch_run_cmds_parallel(cmds: List[str], timeout_seconds: int = 360, max_workers: int = 4) -> Tuple[int, int, int]:
     """
     批量执行命令（并行），每个命令有超时限制

     Args:
         cmds: 命令列表
         timeout_seconds: 每个命令的超时时间（秒），默认 360 秒（3 分钟）
         max_workers: 最大并行进程数，默认 4

     Returns:
         (success_count, failed_count, timeout_count)
     """
     from concurrent.futures import ProcessPoolExecutor, as_completed

     print("\n" + "=" * 60)
     print("开始并行执行命令")
     print("=" * 60)
     print("命令数量: {}".format(len(cmds)))
     print("最大并行数: {}".format(max_workers))
     print("每个命令超时: {} 秒".format(timeout_seconds))
     print("")

     success_count = 0
     failed_count = 0
     timeout_count = 0

     with ProcessPoolExecutor(max_workers=max_workers) as executor:
         # 提交所有任务
         future_to_cmd = {
             executor.submit(run_single_cmd, cmd, timeout_seconds): cmd for cmd in cmds
         }

         # 等待任务完成
         for future in as_completed(future_to_cmd):
             try:
                 cmd, success, message = future.result()
                 if success:
                     success_count += 1
                     print("[✓] 完成")
                 else:
                     failed_count += 1
                     if message == "超时":
                         timeout_count += 1
                     print("[✗] 失败: {}".format(message))
             except Exception as e:
                 failed_count += 1
                 print("[✗] 异常: {}".format(str(e)))

     print("")
     print("=" * 60)
     print("执行完成")
     print("=" * 60)
     print("总数: {}".format(len(cmds)))
     print("成功: {}".format(success_count))
     print("失败: {}".format(failed_count))
     print("超时: {}".format(timeout_count))
     print("")

     return (success_count, failed_count, timeout_count)


 def get_anims(chr_dir: str) -> List[str]:
     # mu = muse_uploader.MuseUploader('svn/svn_sync', 'svn_sync')
     anims: List[str] = []
     for root, dirs, files in os.walk(chr_dir):
         for f in files:
             if f.endswith(".anim"):
                 # ni_name = f.rsplit('.')[0]
                 # result = mu.muse.search_assets(asset_name=ani_name, category_ids=[H74_SVN_DIR_ID])
                 # assets = result['records']
                 # if len(assets) > 0:
                 #     continue
                 f_path = os.path.join(root, f)
                 anims.append(f_path)
     return anims


 def get_skeleton(chr_dirs: str) -> List[str]:
     skeletons: List[str] = []
     for root, dirs, files in os.walk(chr_dirs):
         for f in files:
             if f.endswith(".skeleton"):
                 f_path = os.path.join(root, f)
                 f_path = f_path.replace("\\", "/")
                 skeletons.append(f_path)
     skeletons.sort(key=lambda x: os.path.getsize(x))
     return skeletons


 def get_model_list(model_datas: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]], skeletons: List[str]) -> List[str]:
     model_list: List[str] = []
     for skeleton_path in skeletons:
         skeleton_path = skeleton_path.split("Package/")[-1]
         skeleton_name = skeleton_path.split("/")[1]
         if skeleton_name in model_config.arcolab_models:
             return ["use_arcolab"]

         if skeleton_name in model_config.model_data:
             return model_config.model_data[skeleton_name]

         for _, model_data in model_datas.items():
             if model_data.get("skeleton") != skeleton_path:
                 continue

             meshes = model_data.get("meshes")
             if not meshes:
                 continue

             for mesh in meshes:
                 if "spmodel" in mesh:
                     continue

                 if "test_tixing" not in mesh and not mesh.endswith("_lod0"):
                     mesh += "_lod0"

                 model_list.append(mesh)
     model_list = list(set(model_list))
     return model_list


 def build_export_cmds(skeleton_file: str, model_list: List[str], anim_list: List[str], export_dir: str) -> List[str]:
     """
     构建导出命令（批量模式，多个动画打包成一个命令）

     Args:
         skeleton_file: 骨骼文件路径
         model_list: 模型列表
         anim_list: 动画列表
         export_dir: 导出目录

     Returns:
         命令列表
     """
     if not os.path.exists(export_dir):
         os.makedirs(export_dir)

     # 创建 modellib 批处理文件目录
     temp_dir = os.environ.get("TEMP", os.environ.get("TMP", ""))
     modellib_bat_dir = os.path.join(temp_dir, "H72Messiah_AL_temp", "modellib_bat")
     if not os.path.exists(modellib_bat_dir):
         os.makedirs(modellib_bat_dir)

     cmd_list = []
     anim_chunk_list = []
     anim_chunk = []
     anim_str_count = 0

     for anim_file in anim_list:
         anim_name = os.path.splitext(os.path.basename(anim_file))[0]
         fbx_file = os.path.join(export_dir, anim_name + ".fbx")
         if os.path.exists(fbx_file):
             continue

         anim_chunk.append(anim_name)
         anim_str_count += len(anim_name)

         # windows cmd max str len 8192
         if anim_str_count > 2000:
             anim_chunk_list.append(anim_chunk)
             anim_chunk = []
             anim_str_count = 0

     if anim_chunk:
         anim_chunk_list.append(anim_chunk)

     if len(",".join(model_list)) > 2000:
         model_list = ["use_arcolab"]
         model_config.model_str_oversize = True

     import datetime

     for idx, anim_names in enumerate(anim_chunk_list):
         if "use_arcolab" in model_list:
             export_cmd = (
                 '"D:\programfiles\ModelLib\modellib.exe" --start=Export --FbxDir="{}" --Skeleton="{}"'
                 " --Anims={} --Mode=1"
             ).format(export_dir, skeleton_file, ",".join(anim_names))
         elif model_list:
             # 有模型列表时添加 --Models 参数
             export_cmd = (
                 '"D:\programfiles\ModelLib\modellib.exe" --start=Export --FbxDir="{}" --Skeleton="{}"'
                 " --Models={} --Anims={} --Mode=1"
             ).format(
                 export_dir, skeleton_file, ",".join(model_list), ",".join(anim_names)
             )
         else:
             # 没有模型列表时不添加 --Models 参数
             export_cmd = (
                 '"D:\programfiles\ModelLib\modellib.exe" --start=Export --FbxDir="{}" --Skeleton="{}"'
                 " --Anims={} --Mode=1"
             ).format(export_dir, skeleton_file, ",".join(anim_names))
         export_cmd = export_cmd.replace("\\", "/")
         print("\nexport_cmd\n", export_cmd)

         # 保存命令到批处理文件
         timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S_%f")
         bat_filename = f"modellib_batch_{idx + 1}_{timestamp}.bat"
         bat_path = os.path.join(modellib_bat_dir, bat_filename)

         # 提取路径信息用于注释
         skeleton_name = os.path.basename(os.path.dirname(skeleton_file))
         models_info = (
             ",".join(model_list)
             if model_list and "use_arcolab" not in model_list
             else "无（仅导出骨骼动画）"
         )
         anim_names_preview = ", ".join(anim_names[:5]) + (
             "..." if len(anim_names) > 5 else ""
         )

         bat_content = f"""@echo off
 chcp 65001 >nul
 REM ========================================
 REM ModelLib 批量动画导出批处理文件
 REM ========================================
 REM 
 REM 生成时间: {datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")}
 REM 批次编号: {idx + 1}
 REM 
 REM ========================================
 REM 导出信息
 REM ========================================
 REM 骨骼名称: {skeleton_name}
 REM 动画数量: {len(anim_names)}
 REM 动画列表: {anim_names_preview}
 REM 模型列表: {models_info}
 REM 
 REM ========================================
 REM 路径信息
 REM ========================================
 REM 骨骼文件: {skeleton_file}
 REM 导出目录: {export_dir}
 REM 
 REM ========================================
 REM 使用注意事项
 REM ========================================
 REM 1. 如果遇到权限错误，请右键此文件选择"以管理员身份运行"
 REM 2. 确保 ModelLib 已正确安装在 D:\programfiles\ModelLib
 REM 3. 确保骨骼文件和动画文件存在且路径正确
 REM 4. 批量导出可能需要较长时间，请耐心等待
 REM 5. 导出过程中请勿关闭此窗口
 REM 6. 如果遇到 _readResource 错误，通常不影响导出结果
 REM 
 REM ========================================
 REM 参数说明
 REM ========================================
 REM --start=Export    : 启动导出功能
 REM --FbxDir          : FBX 文件输出目录
 REM --Skeleton        : 骨骼文件路径
 REM --Models          : 模型列表（逗号分隔，可选）
 REM --Anims           : 动画名称列表（逗号分隔）
 REM --Mode=1          : 导出模式（1=标准模式）
 REM 
 REM ========================================

 echo 开始批量导出动画
 echo 骨骼: {skeleton_name}
 echo 动画数量: {len(anim_names)}
 echo 模型: {models_info}
 echo.

 {export_cmd}

 if %errorlevel% neq 0 (
     echo.
     echo ========================================
     echo 批量导出失败
     echo ========================================
     echo 错误代码: %errorlevel%
     echo 请检查上方的错误信息
     echo.
     pause
     exit /b 1
 )

 echo.
 echo ========================================
 echo 批量导出成功
 echo ========================================
 echo 已导出 {len(anim_names)} 个动画
 echo 输出目录: {export_dir}
 echo.
 pause
 """

         with open(bat_path, "w", encoding="utf-8-sig") as f:
             f.write(bat_content)

         print(f"已保存 modellib 批量命令到: {bat_path}")

         cmd_list.append(export_cmd)
     return cmd_list


 def build_export_cmds_per_anim(
     skeleton_file: str, model_list: List[str], anim_list: List[str], export_dir: str, batch_size: int = 1
 ) -> List[str]:
     """
     构建导出命令（每个命令导出 batch_size 个动画，用于多进程）

     Args:
         skeleton_file: 骨骼文件路径
         model_list: 模型列表
         anim_list: 动画列表
         export_dir: 导出目录
         batch_size: 每个命令导出的动画数量，默认 1

     Returns:
         命令列表（每个命令对应 batch_size 个动画）
     """
     if not os.path.exists(export_dir):
         os.makedirs(export_dir)

     # 创建 modellib 批处理文件目录
     temp_dir = os.environ.get("TEMP", os.environ.get("TMP", ""))
     modellib_bat_dir = os.path.join(temp_dir, "H72Messiah_AL_temp", "modellib_bat")
     if not os.path.exists(modellib_bat_dir):
         os.makedirs(modellib_bat_dir)

     cmd_list = []

     if len(",".join(model_list)) > 2000:
         model_list = ["use_arcolab"]
         model_config.model_str_oversize = True

     # 收集需要导出的动画
     anims_to_export = []
     for anim_file in anim_list:
         anim_name = os.path.splitext(os.path.basename(anim_file))[0]
         fbx_file = os.path.join(export_dir, anim_name + ".fbx")

         # 跳过已存在的 FBX
         if not os.path.exists(fbx_file):
             anims_to_export.append(anim_name)

     # 按 batch_size 分组动画
     for i in range(0, len(anims_to_export), batch_size):
         batch_anims = anims_to_export[i : i + batch_size]
         anims_str = ",".join(batch_anims)

         # 生成批处理文件名
         timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S_%f")
         # 使用第一个动画名或批次编号作为文件名
         first_anim = batch_anims[0] if batch_anims else "unknown"
         if len(batch_anims) > 1:
             bat_filename = (
                 f"modellib_batch_{first_anim}_x{len(batch_anims)}_{timestamp}.bat"
             )
         else:
             bat_filename = f"modellib_{first_anim}_{timestamp}.bat"
         bat_path = os.path.join(modellib_bat_dir, bat_filename)

         # 生成对应的日志文件路径
         log_filename = bat_filename.replace(".bat", ".log")
         log_path = os.path.join(modellib_bat_dir, log_filename)

         # 提取路径信息用于模板变量
         skeleton_name = os.path.basename(os.path.dirname(skeleton_file))
         models_info = (
             ",".join(model_list)
             if model_list and "use_arcolab" not in model_list
             else "无（仅导出骨骼动画）"
         )
         anims_preview = ", ".join(batch_anims[:3]) + (
             "..." if len(batch_anims) > 3 else ""
         )

         # 构建导出命令（使用相对路径modellib.exe，因为批处理文件会先cd到ModelLib目录）
         # 添加 --NotLoadMessiahInfo=1 和 --LogPath 参数
         if "use_arcolab" in model_list:
             export_cmd = (
                 'modellib.exe --start=Export --FbxDir="{}" --Skeleton="{}"'
                 " --Anims={} --Mode=1 --NotLoadMessiahInfo=1 --LogPath=\"%LOG_PATH%\""
             ).format(export_dir, skeleton_file, anims_str)
         elif model_list:
             # 有模型列表时添加 --Models 参数
             export_cmd = (
                 'modellib.exe --start=Export --FbxDir="{}" --Skeleton="{}"'
                 " --Models={} --Anims={} --Mode=1 --NotLoadMessiahInfo=1 --LogPath=\"%LOG_PATH%\""
             ).format(export_dir, skeleton_file, ",".join(model_list), anims_str)
         else:
             # 没有模型列表时不添加 --Models 参数
             export_cmd = (
                 'modellib.exe --start=Export --FbxDir="{}" --Skeleton="{}"'
                 " --Anims={} --Mode=1 --NotLoadMessiahInfo=1 --LogPath=\"%LOG_PATH%\""
             ).format(export_dir, skeleton_file, anims_str)

         export_cmd = export_cmd.replace("\\", "/")

         # 从模板文件读取批处理文件模板
         template_dir = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "bat_template")
         template_file = os.path.join(template_dir, "export_fbx.bat.template")

         if not os.path.exists(template_file):
             raise FileNotFoundError(f"批处理文件模板不存在: {template_file}")

         # 读取模板
         with open(template_file, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
             bat_content = f.read()

         # 替换模板变量
         bat_content = bat_content.replace("{ENABLE_LOG}", "1")
         bat_content = bat_content.replace("{GENERATE_TIME}", datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"))
         bat_content = bat_content.replace("{LOG_PATH}", log_path)
         bat_content = bat_content.replace("{SKELETON_NAME}", skeleton_name)
         bat_content = bat_content.replace("{ANIM_COUNT}", str(len(batch_anims)))
         bat_content = bat_content.replace("{ANIMS_PREVIEW}", anims_preview)
         bat_content = bat_content.replace("{MODELS_INFO}", models_info)
         bat_content = bat_content.replace("{SKELETON_FILE}", skeleton_file)
         bat_content = bat_content.replace("{EXPORT_DIR}", export_dir)
         bat_content = bat_content.replace("{EXPORT_CMD}", export_cmd)
         # 不需要验证块，传入空字符串
         bat_content = bat_content.replace("{FBX_VERIFY_BLOCKS}", "")

         # 写入批处理文件（使用 UTF-8 编码以支持中文，避免BOM问题）
         with open(bat_path, "w", encoding="utf-8", newline='\r\n', errors='replace') as f:
             f.write(bat_content)

         print(f"已保存 modellib 命令到: {bat_path}")

         # 返回命令字符串（用于兼容性，但实际执行的是批处理文件）
         cmd_list.append(export_cmd)

     return cmd_list


 def render_preview(
     fbx_file: str,
     render_root: str,
     skin_file: Optional[str] = None,
     static_ske_mesh_file: Optional[str] = None,
     root_bone: Optional[str] = None,
     debug_mode: bool = False,
     debug_dir: Optional[str] = None,
     camera_offset_x: Optional[float] = None,
     camera_offset_y: Optional[float] = None,
     import_material: bool = True,
     render_width: Optional[int] = None,
     render_height: Optional[int] = None,
     maya_version: str = "maya-2022",
     ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path: Optional[str] = None,
     overwrite_playblast: bool = False,
 ) -> None:
     fbx_file = fbx_file.replace("\\", "/")
     asset_name = fbx_file.split("/")[-3]

     # 如果没有传入 skin_file，使用配置中的默认值
     if skin_file is None:
         skin_file = ""
         if asset_name in model_config.arcolab_models:
             skin_file = model_config.arcolab_models[asset_name]

         if model_config.model_str_oversize:
             skin_file = model_config.defalut_skin

     render_cmd = 'rez env {} maya_pipe ffmpeg_app .use_cloud -c "render_ani_fbx -fbx_file {} -render_dir {}'.format(
         maya_version, fbx_file, render_root
     )
     if skin_file:
         render_cmd += " -skin_file {}".format(skin_file)
     if static_ske_mesh_file:
         render_cmd += " -static_ske_mesh_file {}".format(static_ske_mesh_file)
     if root_bone:
         render_cmd += " -root_bone {}".format(root_bone)
     if debug_mode:
         render_cmd += " -debug_mode"
     if debug_dir:
         render_cmd += " -debug_dir {}".format(debug_dir)
     if camera_offset_x is not None:
         render_cmd += " -camera_offset_x {}".format(camera_offset_x)
     if camera_offset_y is not None:
         render_cmd += " -camera_offset_y {}".format(camera_offset_y)
     if render_width is not None:
         render_cmd += " -render_width {}".format(render_width)
     if render_height is not None:
         render_cmd += " -render_height {}".format(render_height)
     if not import_material:
         render_cmd += " -no_import_material"
     if ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path:
         render_cmd += " -ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path {}".format(ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path)
     if overwrite_playblast:
         render_cmd += " -overwrite_playblast"
     render_cmd += '"'

     print(render_cmd)
     import subprocess

     env = os.environ.copy()
     # 所有 Maya 版本都需要设置 PYTHONIOENCODING=gbk
     # 因为 Windows CMD 默认使用 GBK 编码，即使设置了 chcp 65001
     # Maya 的输出需要与 CMD 的编码匹配
     env["PYTHONIOENCODING"] = "gbk"

     # 使用 PowerShell 运行命令，而不是 cmd.exe
     # PowerShell 对 UTF-8 有更好的支持
     powershell_cmd = ['powershell', '-NoProfile', '-ExecutionPolicy', 'Bypass', '-Command', render_cmd]
     subprocess.call(powershell_cmd, env=env)


 def safe_relpath(path: str, start: str) -> str:
     """
     安全的相对路径计算，处理跨磁盘的情况

     Args:
         path: 目标路径
         start: 起始路径

     Returns:
         str: 相对路径，如果跨磁盘则返回基于路径结构的相对表示
     """
     try:
         return os.path.relpath(path, start)
     except ValueError:
         # 跨磁盘情况：检查是否在同一磁盘
         path_drive = os.path.splitdrive(path)[0]
         start_drive = os.path.splitdrive(start)[0]

         if path_drive != start_drive:
             # 跨磁盘，返回标准化后的路径（使用正斜杠）
             path_normalized = os.path.normpath(path).replace("\\", "/")
             # 如果路径是绝对路径，尝试提取相对部分
             # 否则直接返回标准化路径
             return path_normalized
         else:
             # 同一磁盘但relpath失败，可能是其他原因，返回标准化路径
             return os.path.normpath(path).replace("\\", "/")


 def get_anim_res_from_skeleton(skeleton_file: str) -> List[Any]:
     """
     从.skeleton文件中读取动画的res字段

     Args:
         skeleton_file: .skeleton文件路径

     Returns:
         List[AnimResInfo]: 动画资源信息列表
     """
     try:
         # 使用相对导入避免循环导入
         from .data_structures import AnimResInfo

         tree = ET.parse(skeleton_file)
         root = tree.getroot()

         anim_res_list = []
         for anim in root.iter("anim"):
             name_elem = anim.find("name")
             res_elem = anim.find("res")

             if name_elem is not None and res_elem is not None:
                 anim_name = name_elem.text
                 res_path = res_elem.text
                 if anim_name and res_path:
                     anim_res_info = AnimResInfo(name=anim_name, res=res_path)
                     anim_res_list.append(anim_res_info)

         return anim_res_list
     except Exception as e:
         print(f"解析skeleton文件失败: {skeleton_file}, 错误: {str(e)}")
         return []


 def check_biped(skeleton_file: str) -> bool:
     tree = ET.parse(skeleton_file)
     root = tree.getroot()

     for node in root.iter("node"):
         identifier = node.find("identifier")
         if (
             identifier is not None
             and identifier.text
             and identifier.text.startswith("Bip")
         ):
             return False
     return True


 def get_mp4_file_id(asset: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:  # ⬅️ (第802行) None

 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
 import os
 import shutil
 import sys
 import tempfile

 import pipe.log
 import pipe.config

 from muse_pipe import muse_uploader
 from svn_to_muse import utils

 class CreatePreview(object):
     def __init__(self):
         self.log = pipe.log.setup_default_logger(
             'CreatePreview', 'wuzu/svn_to_muse')
         self.mu = muse_uploader.MuseUploader('svn/simpleaction_action_sync', 'svn_sync')

     def render_review(self,files):
         fbx_file = ''
         for file_path in files:
             if file_path.endswith('fbx'):
                 fbx_file = file_path
                 break
         if not fbx_file:  # 💡 render_review=<function CreatePreview.render_review at 0x000001955E51E5C0> (function)
             raise Exception('fbx file not found')  # ⬅️ (第38行) None

         anim_name, ext = os.path.splitext(os.path.basename(file_path))
         render_root = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(file_path)), 'render')
         utils.render_preview(file_path, render_root)
         mp4_file = os.path.join(render_root, anim_name + '.mp4')

         if not os.path.exists(mp4_file):
             raise Exception('mp4 file not found')
         self.log.info('render mp4: {}'.format(mp4_file))
         return mp4_file

     def run(self,asset_id):
         download_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()
         asset = self.mu.muse.get_asset(asset_id)
         files = self.mu.download(asset_id, download_dir)
         mp4_file = self.render_review(files)

         folder_data = self.mu.upload_files_recursive([mp4_file],[mp4_file])
         asset_data = {
             'attachment_task_list': folder_data,
         }
         self.mu.update_muse_asset(asset, asset_data)
         # clear dir
         shutil.rmtree(download_dir)

 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
 import os.path
 import sys
 import json
 import pipe.log
 import pipe.config
 import pipe.eventlog  # ⬅️ (第21行) None

 import muse_pipe.muse_uploader as muse_uploader
 from svn_to_muse import create_preview
 from svn_to_muse import utils
 from muse_pipe import utils as muse_utils


 class AiVideoTags(object):
     def __init__(self,mu=None):
         self.log = pipe.log.setup_default_logger(
             'AiVideoTags', 'wuzu/svn_to_muse')
         self.mu=mu or muse_uploader.MuseUploader('svn/simpleaction_action_sync', 'svn_sync')

     def run(self,asset_id):
         asset = self.mu.muse.get_asset(asset_id)
         mp4_attachment = utils.get_mp4_file_id(asset)
         if not mp4_attachment:
             cp=create_preview.CreatePreview()
             cp.run(asset_id)
             asset = self.mu.muse.get_asset(asset_id)
             mp4_attachment = utils.get_mp4_file_id(asset)


         if not asset['projVisible']:
             self.mu.update_muse_asset(asset, {"proj_visible":True})

         ai_tag_data = muse_utils.ai_video_tag(asset_id,mp4_attachment['id'],mp4_attachment['filename'])
         ai_tags = ai_tag_data['action_tags']
         ai_tags.extend(ai_tag_data['emotion_tags'])
         ai_tags.extend(ai_tag_data['name_tags'])
         ai_tags = list(set(ai_tags))
         self.log.info("AI tags: {}".format(ai_tags))

         asset_data = {
             "description_multil": {"zh_CN": ai_tag_data.get("action_summary")},
             "ai_prompt": ai_tag_data.get("action_summary"),
             "ai_tags": ai_tags,
             "ai_tags_multi": [{"name_multi": {"zh_CN": tag}, "name": tag} for tag in ai_tags],
             "common": {"custom_tags": [asset['category_names'][-1],'ai_tags']},
         }

         #self.log.info("Asset data updated: {}".format(asset_data))
         self.mu.update_muse_asset(asset, asset_data)

         pipe.eventlog.count_me('wuzu/svn_to_muse',
                                'ai_tags')

     def upload_muse(self, file_path: str, anim_data: Optional[Any] = None) -> None:  # 💡 self=<__main__.FbxToMuse object at 0x000001955E606610>, file_path='D:\\TD_Depot\\Wuzu_dev\\test_export\\Char\\a_03_common_boy\\common_boy\\anims\\HIT_L_to_R_02.fbx', anim_data=None
         anim_name, ext = os.path.splitext(os.path.basename(file_path))  # 💡 anim_name='HIT_L_to_R_02' (str), ext='.fbx' (str)
         render_root = os.path.join(
             os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(file_path)), "render"
         )
         # 如果不跳过渲染，则调用 Maya 渲染  # 💡 render_root='D:\\TD_Depot\\Wuzu_dev\\test_export\\Char\\a_03_common_boy\\common_boy\\render' (str)
         if not self.skip_render:
             utils.render_preview(
                 file_path,
                 render_root,
                 skin_file=self.fbx_config.skin_file,
                 static_ske_mesh_file=self.fbx_config.static_ske_mesh_file,
                 root_bone=self.fbx_config.root_bone,
                 debug_mode=self.render_config.debug_mode,
                 debug_dir=self.render_config.debug_dir,
                 camera_offset_x=self.render_config.camera_offset_x,
                 camera_offset_y=self.render_config.camera_offset_y,
                 import_material=self.render_config.import_material,
                 render_width=self.render_config.render_width,
                 render_height=self.render_config.render_height,
                 maya_version=self.maya_version,
                 ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path=self.fbx_config.ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path,
                 overwrite_playblast=self.render_config.overwrite_playblast,
             )
         else:
             lprint("Skipping Maya render, using existing preview files")
             print("Skipping Maya render, using existing preview files")

         mp4_file = os.path.join(render_root, anim_name + ".mp4")
         gif_file = os.path.join(render_root, anim_name + ".gif")
         if not os.path.exists(mp4_file):
             raise Exception("render file not found: {}".format(mp4_file))
         if not os.path.exists(gif_file):
             raise Exception("render file not found: {}".format(gif_file))

         # 如果跳过 muse 上传，只做拍屏
         if self.skip_upload_muse:
             lprint("skip muse upload, render done: {}".format(mp4_file))
             print("render done: {}".format(mp4_file))
             print("render done: {}".format(gif_file))
             return

         # 上传文件列表：永远只上传 mesh_ani_fbx_path（ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path）
         if not self.fbx_config.ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path:
             raise Exception("ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path is required for upload_muse")
         if not os.path.exists(self.fbx_config.ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path):
             raise Exception("ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path not found: {}".format(self.fbx_config.ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path))

         upload_fbx_path = self.fbx_config.ske_mesh_ani_fbx_path
         upload_files = [upload_fbx_path]

         file_size = os.path.getsize(upload_fbx_path) / 1024
         lprint(f"[upload_muse] 准备上传文件: {upload_fbx_path} ({file_size:.2f} KB)")

         file_path = file_path.replace("\\", "/")
         upload_fbx_path = upload_fbx_path.replace("\\", "/")
         #category_list = [self.mu.category_root, "Char"]
         category_list = ["svn", "Char"]#暂时

         # 根据 hierarchy_template 参数构建层级（跳过anims层级）
         # 路径格式：Char/角色/骨骼/anims/动画.fbx
         # 模板示例：
         #   "" 或空: [category_root, "Char"]
         #   "{char_name}": [category_root, "Char", "角色"]
         #   "{char_name}/{skeleton_name}": [category_root, "Char", "角色", "骨骼"]（默认，推荐）
         # hierarchy_template 的层级解析基于“上传用FBX路径”
         if "Char/" in upload_fbx_path and self.muse_config.hierarchy_template:
             path_items = upload_fbx_path.split("Char/")[-1].split("/")
             # 移除"anims"层级和.fbx文件名
             path_items = [item for item in path_items if item != "anims" and not item.endswith(".fbx")]
             # 解析模板
             template = self.muse_config.hierarchy_template.strip()
             if template:
                 # 如果模板包含变量占位符，进行替换
                 if "{" in template:
                     # 构建变量字典
                     # 路径格式：Char/角色/骨骼/anims/动画.fbx
                     # path_items[0] = 角色, path_items[1] = 骨骼
                     var_dict = {}
                     if len(path_items) > 0:
                         var_dict['char_name'] = path_items[0]
                     if len(path_items) > 1:
                         var_dict['skeleton_name'] = path_items[1]
                     if len(path_items) > 2:
                         var_dict['extra'] = path_items[2]
                     formatted = template.format(**var_dict)
                     # 按斜杠分割，添加到category_list
                     category_list.extend([p.strip() for p in formatted.split("/") if p.strip()])

                 else:
                     # 如果模板不包含占位符，直接按斜杠分割
                     category_list.extend([p.strip() for p in template.split("/") if p.strip()])

         # 获取要上传的标签（写入资产，但不用于判定是否存在）
         tags = self.muse_config.custom_tags or []

         # 只按名称查找是否存在同名资产（不比较标签）
         result = self.mu.muse.search_assets(asset_name=anim_name, page_size=1000)
         assets = result.get('records', [])

         is_update = bool(assets)
         existing_asset = assets[0] if assets else None

         category_list = [c for c in category_list if c]
         # 尝试自动创建Muse分类目录
         try:
             lprint(f"[upload_muse] 开始检查/创建分类目录: {category_list}")
             self._ensure_category_exists(category_list)
             lprint(f"[upload_muse] 分类目录检查完成")
         except Exception as e:
             import traceback as _tb
             error_str = str(e)
             lprint(f"[upload_muse] 创建分类目录失败: {error_str}")
             lprint(_tb.format_exc())
             if "同级同名目录" in error_str:
                 raise RuntimeError(
                     f"Muse分类目录创建失败：服务器存在同名目录冲突。\n"
                     f"请登录Muse后台，在对应分类下删除重复的同名目录后重试。\n"
                     f"原始错误: {error_str}"
                 ) from e
         category_name = ",".join(category_list)

         folder_data = self.mu.upload_files_recursive(upload_files, upload_files)
         thumbnail_data = self.mu.upload_files_recursive([gif_file], [gif_file])

         action = "更新" if is_update else "创建"
         asset_id = existing_asset.get('id') if is_update else "新资产"
         lprint(f"[upload_muse] {action}资产: name={anim_name}, category={category_name}, id={asset_id}")

         # 标签已在上面获取，直接使用

         # 获取简介（仅从AnimData中获取）
         description = ""
         if anim_data and hasattr(anim_data, 'description'):
             description = anim_data.description or ""

         data = {
             "attachment_task_list": folder_data,
             "cover_attachment_task_list": thumbnail_data,
             "categoryName": category_name,
             "proj_visible": True,
             "name_multil": {
                 "zh_CN": anim_name,
             },
             "common": {"custom_tags": tags},
         }

         # 如果有简介，添加到data中
         if description:
             data["description_multil"] = {
                 "zh_CN": description
             }

         lprint("="*60)
         if is_update:
             lprint("准备更新现有 Muse 资产")
             lprint(f"资产ID: {existing_asset.get('id')}")
         else:
             lprint("准备创建新 Muse 资产")
         lprint(f"动画名称: {anim_name}")
         lprint(f"分类名称: {category_name}")
         lprint(f"标签: {tags}")
         lprint(f"文件数量: {len(upload_files)}")
         lprint(f"完整 data 结构:")
         lprint(data)
         lprint("="*60)

         try:
             if is_update:
                 # 更新现有资产
                 lprint(f"[upload_muse] 正在更新资产: id={existing_asset.get('id')}, name={anim_name}")
                 asset_info = self.mu.update_muse_asset(existing_asset, data)
                 lprint(f"[upload_muse] update_muse_asset 返回结果: {str(asset_info)[:500]}")
                 print(f"✓ 资产已更新: {anim_name}")
             else:
                 # 创建新资产
                 lprint(f"[upload_muse] 正在创建新资产: name={anim_name}, category={category_name}")
                 asset_info = self.mu.create_muse_asset(data=data)
                 lprint(f"[upload_muse] create_muse_asset 返回结果: {str(asset_info)[:500]}")
                 print(f"✓ 资产已创建: {anim_name}")
         except Exception as e:
             import traceback
             lprint(f"[upload_muse] {'更新' if is_update else '创建'}资产失败: {anim_name}")
             lprint(f"[upload_muse] 错误: {str(e)}")
             lprint(f"[upload_muse] categoryName: {category_name}")
             lprint(f"[upload_muse] 标签: {tags}")
             traceback.print_exc()
             raise
         return
         # update ai tags
         avt = ai_tags.AiVideoTags(self.mu)
         avt.run(asset_info["id"])
         pipe.eventlog.count_me("wuzu/svn_to_muse", "fbx_to_muse")

import re, json

# 读取文件
with open("trace.md", "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    content = f.read()

# 提取 JSON 索引
match = re.search(r'<<<JSON_INDEX>>>\s*```json\s*\n(.*?)\n```', content, re.DOTALL)
if match:
    data = json.loads(match.group(1))
    print(f"版本: {data['version']}")
    print(f"总调用: {data['metadata']['total_calls']}")
    print(f"最大深度: {data['metadata']['max_depth']}")
